<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>казачо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazačók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>казачка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>казачки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>казачко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>kazachok, kozachok <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">dance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (young, little) Cossack <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">can also be condescending</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boy servant</li></ol>

***казенный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казенный.html>казённый</a> (3583)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казна.html>казна́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; derived as if <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казна.html>казна́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> had a reducible stem, with hypothetical unreduced genitive plural <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*казён</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*kazjón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (in fact, the noun has no genitive plural).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казенный.html>казённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> state, government</li>
<li>official, public</li>
<li>formal, perfunctory</li>
<li>commonplace</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> breech (of a rifle)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казна.html>казна́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kazná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казенник.html>казённик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kazjónnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***казна.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казна.html>казна</a> (7335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from a Kypchak Turkic source, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kipchak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kipchak language">Kipchak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="qwm">qazna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasury</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Codex Cumanicus, <i>Ave, porta paradisi</i>, verse 75), further origin uncertain but probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iranian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Iranian languages">Iranian</a></span>, possibly ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Median_language" class="extiw" title="w:Median language">Old Median</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="xme-old">*ganza-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Directly attested since 1389 (treaty of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dmitry_Donskoy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dmitry Donskoy">Dmitry Donskoy</a> with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vladimir_the_Bold" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vladimir the Bold">Vladimir the Bold</a>) while its derivative <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казначей.html>казначе́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaznačéj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used already in the last will of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ivan_II_of_Moscow" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ivan II of Moscow">Ivan II of Moscow</a> circa 1358.
</p><p>Formally close cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nogai_language" class="extiw" title="w:Nogai language">Nogai</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="nog"><a href = vnd.unilang:казна.html>казна</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="nog-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bashkir_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bashkir language">Bashkir</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ba">ҡаҙна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ba-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qaðna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ossetian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ossetian language">Ossetian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="os">хъӕзна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="os-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qæzna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chechen_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chechen language">Chechen</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ce">хазна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ce-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">χazna</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasure, treasury</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ха̏зна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasury; cash register</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">хазна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hazna</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasure; cash register</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romanian language">Romanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">hazna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasury; septic tank</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">hazne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasury</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">خَزْنَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḵazna</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">[a] safe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Also compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">خزینه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hazîne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crimean_Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Crimean Tatar language">Crimean Tatar</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="crh">hazine</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">хәзинә</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xäzinä</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasure, treasury</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">خزینه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xazine</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">خَزِينَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḵazīna</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasury</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γάζα</i> <span href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Persian" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Persian">Middle Persian</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="pal-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ganǰ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">گنج</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren title="w:Sogdian language">Sogdian</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sog-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">γznyʼ</span> <span class="ts mention-ts Latn">/γaznyā/</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasury</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parthian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Parthian language">Parthian</a></span> <i class="Mani mention" lang="xpr">𐫃𐫉𐫗𐫁𐫡</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xpr-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gznbr</span> <span class="ts mention-ts annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казна.html>казна́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казна.html>казны́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казна.html>казны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казна.html>казн</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>treasury, exchequer</li>
<li>fisc</li></ol>

***казнить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казнить.html>казни́ть</a> (6337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казнить.html>казни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kaznítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to execute, to put to death</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to torture, to scourge, to castigate, to punish</li></ol>

***как.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> (14)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kako</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kak</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>how
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лал</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kak</b> on éto sdélal?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How did he do it?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kak</b> delá?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How are things?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пройти.html>пройти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>по́чту</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kak</b> projtí na póčtu?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Can you tell me the way to the post office?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зову́т</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kak</b> vas zovút?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What is your name? (lit. “How do they call you?”)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>what
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́ша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фамилия.html>фами́лия</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kak</b> váša famílija?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What is your surname?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kak</b> on skazál?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What did he say?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">concessive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> as, however much
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1872</b>,  Николай Семёнович <a href = vnd.unilang:лесок.html>Леско́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nikolai_Leskov" class="extiw" title="w:Nikolai Leskov">Nikolai Semyonovich Leskov</a>),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%A1%D0%BE%D0%B1%D0%BE%D1%80%D1%8F%D0%BD%D0%B5_(%D0%9B%D0%B5%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Соборяне (Лесков)">Соборяне</a></cite>, part 4, chapter 6 |  translated as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isabel_Florence_Hapgood" class="extiw" title="w:Isabel Florence Hapgood">Isabel Hapgood</a>, transl., <cite>The Cathedral Folk</cite>, London, 1924, page 88:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упрашивать.html>упра́шивали</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a> что́-нибудь <a href = vnd.unilang:выпить.html>вы́пить</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просьба.html>про́сьбы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвечать.html>отвеча́л</a>:<br />— <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>Нет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:освободить.html>освободи́те</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ровно.html>ро́вно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ровно.html>ро́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вина́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:никакой.html>никако́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пью́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kak</b> jevó ni uprášivali xotʹ štó-nibudʹ výpitʹ, on na vse prósʹby otvečál:<br />— Net, net, osvobodíte! Ja róvno, róvno viná nikakóvo ne pʹju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Urge him <b>as</b> they would to drink something, he replied to all entreaties:<br />"No, no, release me! <li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1982</b>,  Сергей Донатович Довлатов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sergei_Dovlatov" class="extiw" title="w:Sergei Dovlatov">Sergei Donatovich Dovlatov</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:зона.html>Зо́на</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:записка.html>Запи́ски</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надзиратель.html>надзира́теля</a>)</cite> |  translated as Anne Frydman, transl., <cite>The Zone: A Prison Camp Guard's Story</cite>, A.A. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каковой.html>каково́й</a> (8752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кал.html>кал</a> (14082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">калъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kalŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mud, muddy puddle, scum, sewage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kalъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mud, swamp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кал.html>кал</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kal</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кал.html>ка́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кал.html>ка́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кал.html>ка́лов</a></b>)

***калач.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:калач.html>кала́ч</a> (18222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кола́ч</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koláč</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (through akanye), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kolačь</i>, a derivation of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kolo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">circle, wheel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колесо.html>колесо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolesó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ач</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ač</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">кола́ч</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koláč</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">кола́ч</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koláč</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">kòlač</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">koláč</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">koláč</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kołacz</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калека.html>кале́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kaléka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калека.html>кале́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калека.html>кале́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калека.html>кале́к</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:календарь.html>календа́рь</a> (7147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kalendarz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">kalendārium</i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">calendar</i>.
</p>

***каленый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каленый.html>калёный</a> (20498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каленый.html>калёный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kaljónyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>red-hot, tempered (of iron), made from tempered steel
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1899</b>,  A. V. Zheleznova,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oy,_to_ne_vecher" class="extiw" title="w:Oy, to ne vecher"><a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>Сон</a> Стеньки Разина</a>”, in  <cite>Songs of the Ural Cossacks</cite>, 19th-century Russian folk song:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ой.html>Ой́</a>, разы́пались <b>калёныя</b> стрѣ́лы / какъ <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> ма́тушкѣ <a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыро́й</a> землѣ́."</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oj, razýpalisʹ <b>kaljónyja</b> strě́ly / kak po mátuškě syrój zemlě́."</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Ah, the <b>tempered</b> arrows were scattered / as on damp mother earth.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>roasted
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каленый.html>калёные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:орех.html>оре́хи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kaljónyje</b> oréxi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">roasted nuts</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кали́льный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kalílʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кали́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:калечить.html>кале́чить</a> (19047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калека.html>кале́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaléka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калечить.html>кале́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kaléčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покалечить.html>покале́чить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искалечить.html>искале́чить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to maim, to cripple, to mutilate</li>
<li>to pervert, to twist, to warp</li></ol>

***калитка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:калитка.html>кали́тка</a> (3588)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, most likely from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*<a href = vnd.unilang:колит.html>коли́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*kolita</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">door</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/akanye" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:akanye">akanye</a>, where <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*<a href = vnd.unilang:колит.html>коли́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*kolita</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> comes from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>кол</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kol</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stake, peg</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and its original meaning was "equipped with pegs".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калитка.html>кали́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kalítka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калитка.html>кали́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калитка.html>кали́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:калитка.html>кали́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>small door in a fence; wicket gate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садовый.html>садо́вая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:калитка.html>кали́тка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sadóvaja <b>kalítka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">garden gate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a small pie</li></ol>
